                                             AmtLoc:=(AmountLoc*WHTPercentageLoc)/100;

                                         END
                                     ELSE
                                         BEGIN
                                          AmountLoc:=SalesLineLoc."WHT Absorb Base";
                                          AmtLoc:=(AmountLoc*WHTPercentageLoc)/100;
                                         END;
                                      Amount1Loc+=AmtLoc;

                                     END;

                                      A := SalesLineLoc."Line Amount";
                                      IF (SalesLineLoc."VAT %" = 100) THEN BEGIN
                                      SalesLineLoc."Tax Amount (VAT)":=0;
                                      B := SalesLineLoc."Tax Amount (VAT)";
                                      END
                                      ELSE
                                      B:=SalesLineLoc."Tax Amount (VAT)";

                                      VarSlipAmount := VarSlipAmount+A+B;


                                    //VarSlipAmount:=VarSlipAmount + SalesLineLoc."Line Amount"+"Sales Line"."Tax Amount (VAT)"-AmtLoc;

                                    UNTIL SalesLineLoc.NEXT = 0;

                                  //VarSlipAmount:=VarSlipAmount+"Sales Line"."Line Amount"+"Sales Line"."Tax Amount (VAT)"+TotalCustOriginal;
                                  //NK.end

                                  IF ("Sales Header"."Currency Code"<>'') THEN
                                  //VarSlipAmountLCY:=VarSlipAmountLCY+Tot_Exchng_LCy_Dr + Tot_Cust_LCY+Tot_WHT_LCY+Tot_Exchng_LCy_Cr+TotalCustLocal +
                                                                      //Tot_Exchng_LCy_Dr_1 + Tot_Exchng_LCy_Cr_1
                                  VarSlipAmountLCY := VarSlipAmountLCY + Tot_Amt_LCY + Tot_TAX_LCY + Tot_Exchng_LCy_Dr_1 + Tot_Exchng_LCy_Dr + TotalCustLocal - SalesDiscountLCY
                                  ELSE

                                  //nk.begin
                                  //VarSlipAmountLCY:=VarSlipAmountLCY+"Sales Line"."Line Amount"+"Sales Line"."Tax Amount (VAT)"+TotalCustOriginal;
                                  VarSlipAmountLCY:= VarSlipAmount;
                                  //nk.end
                                  //YIMMDEVIP1.0.end

                                  "Sales Header".MODIFY;



                                  //Don't need to write it again for who has created Invoice.Already coded for it above on sales header (OnAfterGetRecord)
                                  {
                                  //==============Sales Header - Footer 5

                                  {
                                  user1.SETRANGE(user1."User ID",USERID);
                                  IF user1.FINDFIRST THEN
                                   Uname1:=user1.Name;
                                   }

                                  //YIMMDEVIP1.0.begin
                                  User1.RESET;
                                  User1.SETRANGE("User Name",'%1',"Sales Header".UID);
                                  IF User1.FINDFIRST THEN
                                   Uname1:=User1."Full Name";
                                  //YIMMDEVIP1.0.end


                                  }

                                  {//UPG13R2DEV
                                  IF (COMPANYNAME = MasterSetup1."Company Name TBI") THEN
                                    HSection5:=FALSE;

                                  IF (COMPANYNAME = MasterSetup1."Company Name YEID") THEN
                                    TextForSignature:='Purchase / Marketing'
                                  ELSE
                                    TextForSignature:='Purchase';
                                  }


                                  //=============Sales Header - Footer 6

                                  IF (COMPANYNAME <> MasterSetup1."Company Name TBI") THEN
                                    HSection6:=FALSE;








                                  END;





                                  //zz


                                  //Message('OnAfter...'+format(TotalCustLocal)+' '+format(WHT_LCY)+' '+format(Tot_Cust_LCY));
                                END;

               DataItemLink=Document No.=FIELD(No.) }

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function
